class="categoryLinkLabel_W154">Tutorials</span></a><button aria-label="Expand sidebar category &#x27;Tutorials&#x27;" aria-expanded="false" type="button" class="clean-btn menu__caret"></button></div></li></ul></nav><button type="button" title="Collapse sidebar" aria-label="Collapse sidebar" class="button button--secondary button--outline collapseSidebarButton_PEFL"><svg width="20" height="20" aria-hidden="true" class="collapseSidebarButtonIcon_kv0_"><g fill="#7a7a7a"><path d="M9.992 10.023c0 .2-.062.399-.172.547l-4.996 7.492a.982.982 0 01-.828.454H1c-.55 0-1-.453-1-1 0-.2.059-.403.168-.551l4.629-6.942L.168 3.078A.939.939 0 010 2.528c0-.548.45-.997 1-.997h2.996c.352 0 .649.18.828.45L9.82 9.472c.11.148.172.347.172.55zm0 0"></path><path d="M19.98 10.023c0 .2-.058.399-.168.547l-4.996 7.492a.987.987 0 01-.828.454h-3c-.547 0-.996-.453-.996-1 0-.2.059-.403.168-.551l4.625-6.942-4.625-6.945a.939.939 0 01-.168-.55 1 1 0 padding-bottom--lg"><div class="row"><div class="col docItemCol_z5aJ"><div class="docItemContainer_c0TR"><article><nav class="theme-doc-breadcrumbs breadcrumbsContainer_Z_bl" aria-label="Breadcrumbs"><ul class="breadcrumbs"><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/configuration"><span>How-to: Configure Weaviate</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item"><a class="breadcrumbs__link" href="/weaviate/configuration/rbac"><span>RBAC</span></a></li><li class="breadcrumbs__item breadcrumbs__item--active"><span class="breadcrumbs__link">Manage roles</span></li></ul></nav><div class="tocCollapsible_ETCw theme-doc-toc-mobile tocMobile_ITEo"><button type="button" class="clean-btn tocCollapsibleButton_TO0P">On this page</button></div><div class="theme-doc-markdown markdown"><header><h1>Manage roles</h1></header><div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-info admonition_xJq3 alert alert--info"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 14 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M7 2.3c3.14 0 5.7 2.56 5.7 5.7s-2.56 5.7-5.7 5.7A5.71 5.71 0 0 1 1.3 8c0-3.14 2.56-5.7 5.7-5.7zM7 1C3.14 1 0 4.14 0 8s3.14 7 7 7 7-3.14 7-7-3.14-7-7-7zm1 3H6v5h2V4zm0 6H6v2h2v-2z"></path></svg></span>Added in <code>v1.29</code></div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><p>Role-based access control (RBAC) is generally available in Weaviate from version <code>v1.29</code>.</p></div></div>
<p>In Weaviate, Role-based access control (RBAC) allows you to define roles and assign permissions to those roles. Users can then be assigned to roles and inherit the permissions associated with those roles.</p>
<p>On this page, you will find examples of how to <strong>manage roles and permissions</strong> with Weaviate client libraries.</p>
<!-- -->
<div class="theme-admonition theme-admonition-tip admonition_xJq3 alert alert--success"><div class="admonitionHeading_Gvgb"><span class="admonitionIcon_Rf37"><svg viewBox="0 0 12 16"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M6.5 0C3.48 0 1 2.19 1 5c0 .92.55 2.25 1 3 1.34 2.25 1.78 2.78 2 4v1h5v-1c.22-1.22.66-1.75 2-4 .45-.75 1-2.08 1-3 0-2.81-2.48-5-5.5-5zm3.64 7.48c-.25.44-.47.8-.67 1.11-.86 1.41-1.25 2.06-1.45 3.23-.02.05-.02.11-.02.17H5c0-.06 0-.13-.02-.17-.2-1.17-.59-1.83-1.45-3.23-.2-.31-.42-.67-.67-1.11C2.44 6.78 2 5.65 2 5c0-2.2 2.02-4 4.5-4 1.22 0 2.36.42 3.22 1.19C10.55 2.94 11 3.94 11 5c0 .66-.44 1.78-.86 2.48zM4 14h5c-.23 1.14-1.3 2-2.5 2s-2.27-.86-2.5-2z"></path></svg></span>Follow these general steps to configure RBAC:</div><div class="admonitionContent_BuS1"><ol><li class="inline-content"><i class="fa-solid fa-key icon-list" style="margin-right:0.5rem"></i><p><b>Step 1.</b> Connect to Weaviate with a user possessing<!-- --> </p><b><a href="/weaviate/configuration/rbac/manage-roles#requirements"><p>role management permissions</p></a></b><p>.</p></li><li class="inline-content"><i class="fa-solid fa-user-shield icon-list" style="margin-right:0.5rem"></i><p><b>Step 2.</b> Grant permissions to a<!-- --> </p><b><a href="/weaviate/configuration/rbac/manage-roles#create-new-roles-with-permissions"><p>new role</p></a></b> <p>or an<!-- --> </p><b><a href="/weaviate/configuration/rbac/manage-roles#grant-additional-permissions"><p>existing role</p></a></b><p>.</p></li><li class="inline-content"><i class="fa-solid fa-user-lock icon-list" style="margin-right:0.5rem"></i><b>Step 3.</b> <b><a href="/weaviate/configuration/rbac/manage-users#assign-a-role-to-a-database-user"><p>Assign the role to a user</p></a></b><p>.</p></li></ol></div></div>
<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="requirements">Requirements for managing roles <i class="fa-solid fa-key"></i><a href="#requirements" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to requirements" title="Direct link to requirements" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<p>Role management requires appropriate <code>role</code> resource permissions that can be obtained through:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">A predefined <code>root</code> role when <a class="" href="/deploy/configuration/configuring-rbac">configuring RBAC</a>.</li>
<li class="">A role with <a href="#role-management-permissions" class=""><code>Role Management</code></a> permissions granted.</li>
</ul>

<h2 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="role-management">Role management <i class="fa-solid fa-user-shield"></i><a href="#role-management" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to role-management" title="Direct link to role-management" translate="no">​</a></h2>
<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="create-new-roles-with-permissions">Create new roles with permissions<a href="#create-new-roles-with-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Create new roles with permissions" title="Direct link to Create new roles with permissions" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Permissions for these resource types can be assigned to roles:</p>
<ol>
<li class="">
<p><a href="#role-management-permissions" class=""><strong>Role Management</strong></a></p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p><a href="#user-management-permissions" class=""><strong>User Management</strong></a></p>
</li>
<li class="">
<p><a href="#collections-permissions" class=""><strong>Collections</strong></a> (collection definitions only, data object permissions are separate)</p>
</li>
<li class="">

</li>

</li>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="role-management-permissions">Create a role with <code>Role Management</code> permissions<a href="#role-management-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to role-management-permissions" title="Direct link to role-management-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Create, read, update and delete all roles starting with <code>testRole*</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="user-management-permissions">Create a role with <code>User Management</code> permissions<a href="#user-management-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to user-management-permissions" title="Direct link to user-management-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Create, read, update and delete all users starting with <code>testUser*</code>.</li>
<li class="">Assign and revoke roles to and from users starting with <code>testUser*</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="collections-permissions">Create a role with <code>Collections</code> permissions<a href="#collections-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to collections-permissions" title="Direct link to collections-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Create, read, update and delete all collections starting with <code>TargetCollection</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="tenants-permissions">Create a role with <code>Tenant</code> permissions<a href="#tenants-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to tenants-permissions" title="Direct link to tenants-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Create and delete tenants starting with <code>TargetTenant</code> in collections starting with <code>TargetCollection</code>.</li>
<li class="">Read metadata (like tenant names and status) for tenants starting with <code>TargetTenant</code> in collections starting with <code>TargetCollection</code>.</li>
<li class="">Update the status of tenants starting with <code>TargetTenant</code> in collections starting with <code>TargetCollection</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="data-permissions">Create a role with <code>Data Objects</code> permissions<a href="#data-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to data-permissions" title="Direct link to data-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Create, read, update and delete data from collections starting with <code>TargetCollection</code>.</li>
<li class="">If multi-tenancy is enabled and the <code>tenant</code> filter is set, the permission only applies to tenants starting with <code>TargetTenant</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="backups-permissions">Create a role with <code>Backups</code> permissions<a href="#backups-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to backups-permissions" title="Direct link to backups-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Manage backups for collections starting with <code>TargetCollection</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="clusters-permissions">Create a role with <code>Cluster Data Access</code> permissions<a href="#clusters-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to clusters-permissions" title="Direct link to clusters-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Read cluster metadata.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="nodes-permissions">Create a role with <code>Node Data Access</code> permissions<a href="#nodes-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to nodes-permissions" title="Direct link to nodes-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Read node metadata at the specified verbosity level for collections starting with <code>TargetCollection</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="aliases-permissions">Create a role with <code>Collection Alias</code> permissions<a href="#aliases-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to aliases-permissions" title="Direct link to aliases-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Create, read, update and delete collection aliases starting with <code>TargetAlias</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="replications-permissions">Create a role with <code>Replications</code> permissions<a href="#replications-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to replications-permissions" title="Direct link to replications-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Create, read, update and delete replica movement operations for collections starting with <code>TargetCollection</code> and shards starting with <code>TargetShard</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h4 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="groups-permissions">Create a role with <code>Groups</code> permissions<a href="#groups-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to groups-permissions" title="Direct link to groups-permissions" translate="no">​</a></h4>
<p>This example creates a role called <code>testRole</code> with permissions to:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Read information about and assign/revoke group membership for OIDC groups starting with <code>TargetGroup</code>.</li>
</ul>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="grant-additional-permissions">Grant additional permissions<a href="#grant-additional-permissions" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Grant additional permissions" title="Direct link to Grant additional permissions" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Additional permissions can be granted to a role at any time. The role must already exist.</p>
<p>This example grants additional permissions to the role <code>testRole</code> to:</p>
<ul>
<li class=""><strong>Create new data</strong> in collections that start with <code>TargetCollection</code></li>
</ul>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="remove-permissions-from-a-role">Remove permissions from a role<a href="#remove-permissions-from-a-role" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Remove permissions from a role" title="Direct link to Remove permissions from a role" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Permissions can be revoked from a role at any time. Removing all permissions from a role will delete the role itself.</p>
<p>This example removes the following permissions from the role <code>testRole</code>:</p>
<ul>
<li class="">Read the data from collections that start with <code>TargetCollection</code></li>
<li class="">Create and delete collections that start with <code>TargetCollection</code></li>
</ul>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="list-all-roles">List all roles<a href="#list-all-roles" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to List all roles" title="Direct link to List all roles" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>View all roles in the system and their permissions.</p>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="list-users-with-a-role">List users with a role<a href="#list-users-with-a-role" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to List users with a role" title="Direct link to List users with a role" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>List all users who have the role <code>testRole</code>.</p>

<h3 class="anchor anchorTargetStickyNavbar_Vzrq" id="delete-a-role">Delete a role<a href="#delete-a-role" class="hash-link" aria-label="Direct link to Delete a role" title="Direct link to Delete a role" translate="no">​</a></h3>
<p>Deleting a role will remove it from the system, and revoke the associated permissions from all users who had this role.</p>
